<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports single, multiple, or no selection</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Can be controlled or uncontrolled</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Fully managed keyboard navigation (arrow keys, home, end, etc.)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Vertical and horizontal orientation</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Typeahead to allow focusing the matching item</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports items, labels, groups of items</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports grid and list layouts</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="anatomy" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Anatomy<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#anatomy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Check the listbox anatomy and part names.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute to help identify them in the DOM.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="">No anatomy available for <!-- -->listbox</div>
<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the listbox package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> listbox</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/listbox&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The listbox package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Pass a unique <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">useMachine</code> so generated element ids stay predictable.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>
<div data-scope="tabs" data-part="root" id="tabs:listbox/usage.mdx" data-orientation="horizontal" dir="ltr" class="w_full max-w_768px bd-w_1px my_8 bg_bg.code.block bdr_6px"><div data-scope="tabs" <h3 id="setting-the-initial-selection" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the initial selection<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-initial-selection"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To set the initial selection, you can use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code> property.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>listbox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// ...</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  defaultValue<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;item-1&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">&quot;item-2&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlling-the-selection" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlling the selection<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlling-the-selection"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code> to control selection externally.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>listbox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  value<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;item-1&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">&quot;item-2&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onValueChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { value: string[]; items: CollectionItem[] }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlling-the-highlighted-item" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlling the highlighted item<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlling-the-highlighted-item"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">highlightedValue</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onHighlightChange</code> to control highlighted state.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>listbox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  highlightedValue<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onHighlightChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { highlightedValue: string | null, highlightedItem, highlightedIndex }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">setHighlightedValue</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">highlightedValue</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="filtering" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Filtering<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#filtering"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The listbox component supports filtering of items via <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.getInputProps</code>.
Here&#x27;s an example of how to support searching through a list of items.</p>

<h3 id="selecting-multiple-items" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Selecting multiple items<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#selecting-multiple-items"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To enable multiple selection, set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">selectionMode</code> property to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">multiple</code> or
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">extended</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>listbox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// ...</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  selectionMode<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;multiple&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="selection-modes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Selection Modes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#selection-modes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">selectionMode</code> to control selection behavior:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><strong>single</strong>: A user can select a single item using the space bar, mouse click,
or touch tap.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><strong>multiple</strong>: A user can select multiple items using the space bar, mouse
click, or touch tap to toggle selection on the focused item. Using the arrow
keys, a user can move focus independently of selection.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><strong>extended</strong>: With no modifier keys like <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Ctrl</code>, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Cmd</code> or <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Shift</code>: the
behavior is the same as single selection.</li>
</ul>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>listbox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// ...</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  selectionMode<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;extended&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="selecting-on-highlight" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Selecting on highlight<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#selecting-on-highlight"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">selectOnHighlight</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code> to select items as they become highlighted.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>listbox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  selectOnHighlight<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="disallowing-select-all-shortcuts" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disallowing select-all shortcuts<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disallowing-select-all-shortcuts"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disallowSelectAll</code> to disable <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Cmd/Ctrl + A</code> selection.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>listbox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  selectionMode<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;multiple&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  disallowSelectAll<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-item-selection" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for item selection<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-item-selection"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onSelect</code> to react whenever an item is selected.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>listbox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onSelect</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { value: string }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="disabling-items" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabling items<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabling-items"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To disable an item, you can use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code> property.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getItemProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// ...</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  disabled<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>To disable the entire listbox, you can use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code> property.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>listbox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  disabled<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="grid-layout" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Grid layout<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#grid-layout"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To enable a grid layout, provide a grid collection to the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">collection</code> property.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>listbox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token operator">:</span> listbox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">gridCollection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    items<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    columnCount<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>

<h3 id="horizontal-orientation" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Horizontal orientation<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#horizontal-orientation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">orientation</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">horizontal</code> for horizontal keyboard navigation.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>listbox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  orientation<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;horizontal&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;listbox&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the root part */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;listbox&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;label&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the label part */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;listbox&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the content part */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;listbox&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the item part */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;listbox&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;itemGroup&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the item group part */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="focused-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Focused state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#focused-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The focused state is applied to the item that is currently focused.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;listbox&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-focused</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the focused item part */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="selected-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Selected state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#selected-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The selected state is applied to the item that is currently selected.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;listbox&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-selected</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the selected item part */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>

<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The listbox machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">orientation</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;horizontal&quot; | &quot;vertical&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The orientation of the listbox.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">collection</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">GridCollection&lt;T&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The item collection</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ root: string; content: string; label: string; item: (id: string | number) =&gt; string; itemGroup: (id: string | number) =&gt; string; itemGroupLabel: (id: string | number) =&gt; string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the listbox. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the listbox is disabled</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disallowSelectAll</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to disallow selecting all items when `meta+a` is pressed</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onHighlightChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: HighlightChangeDetails&lt;T&gt;) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">The callback fired when the highlighted item changes.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: ValueChangeDetails&lt;T&gt;) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">The callback fired when the selected item changes.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[]</code><span class="d_block">The controlled keys of the selected items</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[]</code><span class="d_block">The initial default value of the listbox when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the value of the listbox.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">highlightedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The controlled key of the highlighted item</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultHighlightedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The initial value of the highlighted item when opened.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the highlighted value of the listbox.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">loopFocus</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to loop the keyboard navigation through the options</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">selectionMode</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">SelectionMode</code><span class="d_block">How multiple selection should behave in the listbox.

- `single`: The user can select a single item.
- `multiple`: The user can select multiple items without using modifier keys.
- `extended`: The user can select multiple items by using modifier keys.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">scrollToIndexFn</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: ScrollToIndexDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to scroll to a specific index</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">selectOnHighlight</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to select the item when it is highlighted</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">deselectable</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to disallow empty selection</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">typeahead</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to enable typeahead on the listbox</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onSelect</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: SelectionDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when an item is selected</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dir</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;ltr&quot; | &quot;rtl&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The document&#x27;s text/writing direction.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The unique identifier of the machine.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getRootNode</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; ShadowRoot | Node | Document</code><span class="d_block">A root node to correctly resolve document in custom environments. E.x.: Iframes, Electron.</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The listbox <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px value is empty</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">highlightedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The value of the highlighted item</span></li><li class="d_flex prose">highlightedItem</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">V</code><span class="d_block">The highlighted item</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">highlightValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(value: string) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to highlight a value</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">clearHighlightedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Function to clear the highlighted value</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">hasSelectedItems</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether there&#x27;s a selected option</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[]</code><span class="d_block">The selected item keys</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold prose">selectValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(value: string) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to select a value</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Function to select all values.

Otherwise, an exception will be thrown.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(value: string[]) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to set the value of the select</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">clearValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(value?: string) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to clear the value of the select.
If a value is provided, it will only clear that value, otherwise, it will clear all values.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getItemState</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(props: ItemProps&lt;any&gt;) =&gt; ItemState</code><span class="d_block">Returns the state of a select item</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">collection</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">ListCollection&lt;V&gt;</code><span class="d_block">Function to toggle the select</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the select is disabled</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="data-attributes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Data Attributes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#data-attributes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_8px pl_0! li-t_none li-pos_inside dvd-y_1px"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_4 py_4"><div class="fw_semibold">Root</div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_4 max-w_lg"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-scope</kbd></div><span>listbox</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold listbox displays selectable options in single or multiple selection modes.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cresources pkg=\"@zag-js/listbox\"\u003e\n\u003cshowcase package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"listbox/installation.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eAnatomy\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eCheck the listbox anatomy and part functions:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003emachine\u003c/code\u003e - State machine logic.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003econnect\u003c/code\u003e - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003ePass a unique \u003ccode\u003eid\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003edefaultValue\u003c/code\u003e property.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(listbox.machine, {\n  // ...\n  defaultValue: [\"item-1\", \"item-2\"],\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlling the selection\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003evalue\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonValueChange\u003c/code\u003e to control selection externally.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(listbox.machine, {\n  value: [\"item-1\", \"item-2\"],\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string[]; items: CollectionItem[] }\n    console.log(details.value)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlling the highlighted item\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003ehighlightedValue\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonHighlightChange\u003c/code\u003e to control highlighted state.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(listbox.machine, {\n  highlightedValue,\n  onHighlightChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { highlightedValue: string | null, highlightedItem, highlightedIndex }\n    setHighlightedValue(details.highlightedValue)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eFiltering\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe listbox component supports filtering of items via \u003ccode\u003eapi.getInputProps\u003c/code\u003e.\nHere's an example of how to support searching through a list of items.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"listbox/filtering.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSelecting multiple items\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo enable multiple selection, set the \u003ccode\u003eselectionMode\u003c/code\u003e property to \u003ccode\u003emultiple\u003c/code\u003e or\n\u003ccode\u003eextended\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003econst service = \u003ccode\u003eselectionMode\u003c/code\u003e to control selection behavior:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003esingle\u003c/strong\u003e: A user can select a single item using the space bar, mouse click,\nor touch tap.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003emultiple\u003c/strong\u003e: A user can select multiple items using the space bar, mouse\nclick, or touch tap to toggle selection on the focused item. Using the arrow\nkeys, a user can move focus independently of selection.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eextended\u003c/strong\u003e: With no modifier keys like \u003ccode\u003eCtrl\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eCmd\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003eShift\u003c/code\u003e: the\nbehavior is the same as single selectOnHighlight: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eDisallowing select-all shortcuts\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003edisallowSelectAll\u003c/code\u003e to pkg=\"@zag-js/listbox\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"Listbox\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Supports single, multiple, or no selection\n- Can be controlled or uncontrolled\n- Fully managed keyboard navigation (arrow keys, home, end, etc.)\n- Vertical and horizontal orientation\n- Typeahead to allow focusing the matching item\n- Supports items, labels, groups of items\n- Supports grid and list layouts\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the listbox package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"listbox/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nCheck the listbox anatomy and part names.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"listbox\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the listbox package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as listbox from \"@zag-js/listbox\"\n```\n\nThe listbox package exports two key functions:\n\n- `machine` - State machine logic.\n- `connect` - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\n\n\u003e Pass a unique `id` to `useMachine` so generated element ids stay predictable.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"listbox/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Setting the initial selection\n\nTo set the initial selection, you can use the `defaultValue` property.\n\n```tsx\nconst service = useMachine(listbox.machine, {\n  // ...\n  defaultValue: [\"item-1\", \"item-2\"],\n})\n```\n\n### Controlling the selection\n\nUse `value` and `onValueChange` to control selection externally.\n\n```tsx\nconst service = useMachine(listbox.machine, {\n  value: [\"item-1\", \"item-2\"],\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string[]; items: CollectionItem[] }\n    console.log(details.value)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Controlling the highlighted item\n\nUse `highlightedValue` and `onHighlightChange` to control highlighted state.\n\n```tsx\nconst service = useMachine(listbox.machine, {\n  highlightedValue,\n  onHighlightChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { highlightedValue: string | null, highlightedItem, highlightedIndex }\n    setHighlightedValue(details.highlightedValue)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Filtering\n\nThe listbox component supports filtering of items via `api.getInputProps`.\nHere's an example of how to support searching through a list of items.\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"listbox/filtering.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Selecting multiple items\n\nTo enable multiple selection, set the `selectionMode` property to `multiple` or\n`extended`.\n\n```tsx\nconst service = useMachine(listbox.machine, {\n  // ...\n  selectionMode: \"multiple\",\n})\n```\n\n### Selection Modes\n\nUse `selectionMode` to control selection behavior:\n\n- **single**: A user can select a single item using the space bar, mouse click,\n  or touch tap.\n- **multiple**: A user can select multiple items using the space bar, mouse\n  click, or touch tap to toggle selection on the focused item. Using the arrow\n  keys, a user can move focus independently of selection.\n- **extended**: With no modifier keys like `Ctrl`, `Cmd` or `Shift`: the\n  behavior is the same as single selection.\n\n```tsx\nconst service = useMachine(listbox.machine, {\n  // ...\n  selectionMode: \"extended\",\n})\n```\n\n### Selecting on highlight\n\nSet `selectOnHighlight` to `true` to select items as they become highlighted.\n\n```tsx\nconst service = useMachine(listbox.machine, {\n  selectOnHighlight: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Disallowing select-all shortcuts\n\nSet `disallowSelectAll` to disable `Cmd/Ctrl + A` selection.\n\n```tsx\nconst service = useMachine(listbox.machine, {\n  selectionMode: \"multiple\",\n  disallowSelectAll: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for item selection\n\nUse `onSelect` to react whenever an item is selected.\n\n```tsx\nconst service = useMachine(listbox.machine, {\n  onSelect(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string }\n    console.log(details.value)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Disabling items\n\nTo disable an item, you can use the `disabled` property.\n\n```tsx\napi.getItemProps({\n  // ...\n  disabled: true,\n})\n```\n\nTo disable the entire listbox, you can use the `disabled` property.\n\n```tsx\nconst service = useMachine(listbox.machine, {\n  disabled: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Grid layout\n\nTo enable a grid layout, provide a grid collection to the `collection` property.\n\n```tsx\nconst service = useMachine(listbox.machine, {\n  collection: listbox.gridCollection({\n    items: [],\n    columnCount: 3,\n  }),\n})\n```\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"listbox/grid-usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Horizontal orientation\n\nSet `orientation` to `horizontal` for horizontal keyboard navigation.\n\n```tsx\nconst service = useMachine(listbox.machine, {\n  orientation: \"horizontal\",\n  collection,\n})\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n```css\n[data-scope=\"listbox\"][data-part=\"root\"] {\n  /* styles for the root part */\n}\n\n[data-scope=\"listbox\"][data-part=\"label\"] {\n  /* styles for the label part */\n}\n\n[data-scope=\"listbox\"][data-part=\"content\"] {\n  /* styles for the content part */\n}\n\n[data-scope=\"listbox\"][data-part=\"item\"] {\n  /* styles for the item part */\n}\n\n[data-scope=\"listbox\"][data-part=\"itemGroup\"] {\n  /* styles for the item group part */\n}\n```\n\n### Focused state\n\nThe focused state is applied to the item that is currently focused.\n\n```css\n[data-scope=\"listbox\"][data-part=\"item\"][data-focused] {\n  /* styles for the focused item part */\n}\n```\n\n### Selected state\n\nThe selected state is applied to the item that is currently selected.\n\n```css\n[data-scope=\"listbox\"][data-part=\"item\"][data-selected] {\n  /* styles for the selected item part */\n}\n```\n\n### Disabled state\n\nThe disabled state is applied to the item that is currently disabled.\n\n```css\n[data-scope=\"listbox\"][data-part=\"item\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for the disabled item part */\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe listbox machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"listbox\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe listbox `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"listbox\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"listbox\" /\u003e\n\n### CSS Variables\n\n\u003cCssVarTable name=\"listbox\" /\u003e\n\n## Accessibility\n\nAdheres to the\n[Listbox WAI-ARIA design pattern](https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/listbox/)."])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"5:[\"$\",\"$Le\",null,{\"doc\":{\"title\":\"Listbox\",\"description\":\"Used to display a list of
